## <a name="windows-server-2012-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="d1b30-2133">Diritti estesi di Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1b30-2133">Windows Server 2012 Extended Rights</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d1b30-2134">Questa classe contiene i seguenti diritti estesi per Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1b30-2134">This class contains the following extended rights for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
